If not see\n<http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.  */\n\n/* Dead code elimination.\n\n   References:\n\n     Building an Optimizing Compiler,\n     Robert Morgan, Butterworth-Heinemann, 1998, Section 8.9.\n\n     Advanced Compiler Design and Implementation,\n     Steven Muchnick, Morgan Kaufmann, 1997, Section 18.10.\n\n   Dead-code elimination is the removal of statements which have no\n   impact on the program's output.  \"Dead statements\" have no impact\n   on the program's output, while \"necessary statements\" may have\n   impact on the output.\n\n   The algorithm consists of three phases:\n   1. Marking as necessary all statements known to be necessary,\n      e.g. most function calls, writing a value to memory, etc;\n   2. Propagating necessary statements, e.g., the statements\n      giving values to operands in necessary statements; and\n   3. alters the CFG, then it will arrange for the dominators\n   to be recomputed.  */\nstatic bool cfg_altered;\n\n/* When non-NULL holds map from basic block index into the postorder.  */\nstatic int *bb_postorder;\n\n\n/* True if we should treat any stmt with a vdef as necessary.  */\n\nstatic inline bool\nkeep_all_vdefs_p ()\n{\n  return optimize_debug;\n}\n\n/* 1 if CALLEE is the function __cxa_atexit.\n   2 if CALLEE is the function __aeabi_atexit.\n   0 otherwise.   */\n\nstatic inline int\nis_cxa_atexit (const_tree callee)\n{\n  if (callee != NULL_TREE\n      && strcmp (IDENTIFIER_POINTER (DECL_NAME (callee)), \"__cxa_atexit\") == 0)\n    return 1;\n  if (callee != NULL_TREE\n      && strcmp (IDENTIFIER_POINTER (DECL_NAME (callee)), \"__aeabi_atexit\") == 0)\n    return 2;\n  return 0;\n}\n\n/* True if STMT is a call to __cxa_atexit (or __aeabi_atexit)\n   and the function argument to that call is a const  or pure\n   non-looping function decl.  */\n\nstatic inline bool\nis_removable_cxa_atexit_call (gimple *stmt)\n{\n  tree callee = gimple_call_fndecl (stmt);\n  int functype = is_cxa_atexit (callee);\n  if (!functype)\n    return false;\n  if (gimple_call_num_args (stmt) != 3)\n    return false;\n\n  /* The function argument is the 1st argument for __cxa_atexit\n     or the 2nd argument for __eabi_atexit. */\n  tree arg = gimple_call_arg (stmt, functype == 2 ? 1 : 0);\n  if (TREE_CODE (arg) != ADDR_EXPR)\n    return false;\n  arg = TREE_OPERAND (arg, 0);\n  if (TREE_CODE (arg) != FUNCTION_DECL)\n    return false;\n  int flags = flags_from_decl_or_type (arg);\n\n  /* If the function is noreturn then it cannot be removed. */\n  if (flags & ECF_NORETURN)\n    return false;\n\n  /* The function needs to be const or pure and non looping.  */\n  return (flags & (ECF_CONST|ECF_PURE))\n\t  && !(flags & ECF_LOOPING_CONST_OR_PURE);\n}\n\n/* If STMT is not already marked necessary, mark it, and add it to the\n   worklist if ADD_TO_WORKLIST is true.  */\n\nstatic inline void\nmark_stmt_necessary (gimple *stmt, bool add_to_worklist)\n{\n  gcc_assert (stmt);\n\n  if (gimple_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY))\n    return;\n\n  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n    {\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"Marking useful stmt: \");\n      print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, stmt, 0, TDF_SLIM);\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"\\n\");\n    }\n\n  gimple_set_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY, true);\n  if (add_to_worklist)\n    worklist.safe_push (stmt);\n  if (add_to_worklist && bb_contains_live_stmts && !is_gimple_debug (stmt))\n    bitmap_set_bit (bb_contains_live_stmts, gimple_bb (stmt)->index);\n}\n\n\n/* Mark the statement defining operand OP as necessary.  */\n\nstatic inline void\nmark_operand_necessary (tree op)\n{\n  gimple *stmt;\n  int ver;\n\n  gcc_assert (op);\n\n  ver = SSA_NAME_VERSION (op);\n  if (bitmap_bit_p (processed, ver))\n    {\n      stmt = SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (op);\n      gcc_assert (gimple_nop_p (stmt)\n\t\t  || gimple_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY));\n      return;\n    }\n  bitmap_set_bit (processed, ver);\n\n  stmt = SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (op);\n  gcc_assert (stmt);\n\n  if (gimple_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY) || gimple_nop_p (stmt))\n    return;\n\n  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n    {\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"marking necessary through \");\n      print_generic_expr (dump_file, op);\n      fprintf (dump_file, \" stmt \");\n      print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, stmt, 0);\n    }\n\n  gimple_set_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY, true);\n  if (bb_contains_live_stmts)\n    bitmap_set_bit (bb_contains_live_stmts, gimple_bb (stmt)->index);\n  worklist.safe_push (stmt);\n}\n\n/* Return true if STMT is a call to allocation function that can be\n   optimized out if the memory block is never used for anything else\n   than NULL pointer check or free.\n   If NON_NULL_CHECK is false, we can further assume that return value\n   is never checked to be non-NULL.\n   Don't (stmt), a1, a2;\n  if (callee != NULL_TREE\n      && fndecl_built_in_p (callee, BUILT_IN_NORMAL))\n    switch (DECL_FUNCTION_CODE (callee))\n      {\n      case BUILT_IN_MALLOC:\n\targ = 1;\n\tgoto     case BUILT_IN_STRDUP:\n      case BUILT_IN_STRNDUP:\n\targ = 0;\n\t/* FALLTHRU */\n      do_malloc:\n\tif (non_null_check)\n\t  {\n\t    if (flag_malloc_dce <= 1)\n\t      return false;\n\t  }\n\telse if (!flag_malloc_dce)\n\t  return false;\n\tbreak;\n\n      case BUILT_IN_GOMP_ALLOC:\n\targ = 2;\n\tbreak;\n\n      default:;\n      }\n\n  if (arg == -1\n      && callee != NULL_TREE\n      && flag_allocation_dce\n      && gimple_call_from_new_or_delete (stmt)\n      && DECL_IS_REPLACEABLE_OPERATOR_NEW_P (callee))\n    arg = 1;\n\n  switch (arg)\n    {\n    case -1:\n      return false;\n    case 0:\n      return true;\n    case 1:\n    case 2:\n      if (gimple_call_num_args (stmt) < (unsigned) arg)\n\treturn false;\n      a1 = gimple_call_arg (stmt, arg - 1);\n      if (tree_fits_uhwi_p (a1)\n\t  && (tree_to_uhwi (a1)\n\t      > tree_to_uhwi (TYPE_MAX_VALUE (ptrdiff_type_node))))\n\treturn false;\n      return true;\n    case 3:\n      if (gimple_call_num_args (stmt) < 2)\n\treturn false;\n      a1 = gimple_call_arg (stmt, 0);\n      a2 = gimple_call_arg (stmt, 1);\n      if (tree_fits_uhwi_p (a1)\n\t  && (tree_to_uhwi (a1)\n\t      > tree_to_uhwi (TYPE_MAX_VALUE (ptrdiff_type_node))))\n\treturn false;\n      if (tree_fits_uhwi_p (a2)\n\t  && (tree_to_uhwi (a2)\n\t      > tree_to_uhwi (TYPE_MAX_VALUE (ptrdiff_type_node))))\n\treturn false;\n      if (TREE_CODE (a1) == INTEGER_CST\n\t  && TREE_CODE (a2) == INTEGER_CST\n\t  && (wi::to_widest (a1) * wi::to_widest (a2)\n\t      > tree_to_uhwi (TYPE_MAX_VALUE (ptrdiff_type_node))))\n\treturn false;\n      return true;\n    default:\n      gcc_unreachable ();\n    }\n}\n\n/* Return true if STMT is a conditional\n     if (ptr != NULL)\n   where ptr was returned by a removable allocation function.  */\n\nstatic bool\nchecks_return_value_of_removable_allocation_p (gimple *stmt)\n{\n  gcall *def_stmt;\n  return gimple_code (stmt) == GIMPLE_COND\n\t && (gimple_cond_code (stmt) == EQ_EXPR\n\t     || gimple_cond_code (stmt) == NE_EXPR)\n\t && integer_zerop (gimple_cond_rhs (stmt))\n\t && TREE_CODE (gimple_cond_lhs (stmt)) == SSA_NAME\n\t && (def_stmt = dyn_cast <gcall *>\n\t\t\t (SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (gimple_cond_lhs (stmt))))\n\t && is_removable_allocation_p (def_stmt, true);\n}\n\n\n/* Mark STMT as necessary if it obviously is.  Add it to the worklist if\n   it can make other statements necessary.\n\n   If AGGRESSIVE is false, control statements are conservatively marked as\n   necessary.  */\n\nstatic void\nmark_stmt_if_obviously_necessary (gimple *stmt, bool aggressive)\n{\n  /* Statements that are implicitly live.  Most function calls, asm\n     and return statements are required.  Labels and GIMPLE_BIND nodes\n     are kept because they are control flow, and we have no way of\n     knowing whether they can be removed.  DCE can eliminate all the\n     other statements in a block, and CFG can then remove the block\n     and labels.  */\n  switch (gimple_code (stmt))\n    {\n    case GIMPLE_PREDICT:\n    case GIMPLE_LABEL:\n      mark_stmt_necessary (stmt, false);\n      return;\n\n    case GIMPLE_ASM:\n    case GIMPLE_RESX:\n    case GIMPLE_RETURN:\n      mark_stmt_necessary (stmt, true);\n      return;\n\n    case GIMPLE_CALL:\n      {\n\tgcall *call = as_a <gcall *> (stmt);\n\n\t/* Never elide a noreturn call we pruned control-flow for.\n\t   Same for statements that can alter control flow in unpredictable\n\t   ways.  */\n\tif (gimple_call_ctrl_altering_p (call))\n\t  {\n\t    mark_stmt_necessary (call, true);\n\t    return;\n\t  }\n\n\tif (is_removable_allocation_p (call, false))\n\t  return;\n\n\n\t/* For __cxa_atexit calls, don't mark as necessary right away. */\n\tif (is_removable_cxa_atexit_call (call))\n\t  return;\n\n\t/* IFN_GOACC_LOOP calls are necessary in that they are used to\n\t   represent parameter (i.e. step, bound) of a lowered OpenACC\n\t   partitioned loop.  But this kind of partitioned loop might not\n\t   survive from aggressive loop removal for it has loop exit and\n\t   is assumed to be finite.  Therefore, we need to explicitly mark\n\t   these calls. (An example is libgomp.oacc-c-c++-common/pr84955.c) */\n\tif (gimple_call_internal_p (call, IFN_GOACC_LOOP))\n\t  {\n\t    mark_stmt_necessary (call, true);\n\t    return;\n\t  }\n\tbreak;\n      }\n\n    case GIMPLE_DEBUG:\n      /* Debug temps without a value are not useful.  ??? If we could\n\t easily locate the debug temp bind stmt for a use thereof,\n\t would could refrain from marking all debug temps here, and\n\t mark them only if they're used.  */\n      if (gimple_debug_nonbind_marker_p (stmt)\n\t  || !gimple_debug_bind_p (stmt)\n\t  || gimple_debug_bind_has_value_p (stmt)\n\t  || TREE_CODE (gimple_debug_bind_get_var (stmt)) != DEBUG_EXPR_DECL)\n\tmark_stmt_necessary (stmt, false);\n      return;\n\n    case GIMPLE_GOTO:\n      gcc_assert (!simple_goto_p (stmt));\n      mark_stmt_necessary (stmt, true);\n      return;\n\n    case GIMPLE_COND:\n      gcc_assert (EDGE_COUNT (gimple_bb (stmt)->succs) == 2);\n      /* Fall through.  */\n\n    case GIMPLE_SWITCH:\n      if (! aggressive)\n\tmark_stmt_necessary (stmt, true);\n      break;\n\n    case GIMPLE_ASSIGN:\n      /* Mark indirect CLOBBERs to be lazily removed if their SSA operands\n\t do not prevail.  That also makes control flow leading to them\n\t not necessary in aggressive mode.  */\n      if (gimple_clobber_p (stmt) && !zero_ssa_operands (stmt, SSA_OP_USE))\n\treturn;\n      break;\n\n    default:\n      break;\n    }\n\n  /* If the statement has volatile operands, it needs to be preserved.\n     Same for statements that can alter control flow in unpredictable\n     ways.  */\n  if (gimple_has_side_effects (stmt) || is_ctrl_altering_stmt (stmt))\n    {\n      mark_stmt_necessary (stmt, true);\n      return;\n    }\n\n  /* If a statement could throw, it can be deemed necessary unless we\n     are allowed to remove dead EH.  Test this after checking for\n     new/delete operators since we always elide their EH.  */\n  if (!cfun->can_delete_dead_exceptions\n      && stmt_could_throw_p (cfun, stmt))\n    {\n      mark_stmt_necessary (stmt, true);\n      return;\n    }\n\n  if ((gimple_vdef (stmt) && keep_all_vdefs_p ())\n      || stmt_may_clobber_global_p (stmt, false))\n    {\n      mark_stmt_necessary (stmt, true);\n      return;\n    }\n\n  return;\n}\n\n\n/* Mark the last statement of BB as necessary.  */\n\nstatic bool\nmark_last_stmt_necessary (basic_block bb)\n{\n  if (!bitmap_set_bit (last_stmt_necessary, bb->index))\n    return true;\n\n  bitmap_set_bit (bb_contains_live_stmts, bb->index);\n\n  /* We actually mark the statement only if it is a control statement.  */\n  gimple *stmt = *gsi_last_bb (bb);\n  if (stmt && is_ctrl_stmt (stmt))\n    {\n      mark_stmt_necessary (stmt, true);\n      return true;\n    }\n  return false;\n}\n\n\n/* Mark control dependent edges of BB as necessary.  We have to do this only\n   once for each basic block so we set the appropriate bit after we're done.\n\n   When IGNORE_SELF is true, ignore BB in the list of control dependences.  */\n\nstatic void\nmark_control_dependent_edges_necessary (basic_block bb, bool ignore_self)\n{\n  bitmap_iterator bi;\n  unsigned edge_number;\n  bool skipped = false;\n\n  gcc_assert (bb != EXIT_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun));\n\n  if (bb == ENTRY_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun))\n    return;\n\n  EXECUTE_IF_SET_IN_BITMAP (cd->get_edges_dependent_on (bb->index),\n\t\t\t    0, edge_number, bi)\n    {\n      basic_block cd_bb = cd->get_edge_src (edge_number);\n\n      if (ignore_self && cd_bb == bb)\n\t{\n\t  skipped = true;\n\t  continue;\n\t}\n\n      if (!mark_last_stmt_necessary (cd_bb))\n\tmark_control_dependent_edges_necessary (cd_bb, false);\n    }\n\n  if (!skipped)\n    bitmap_set_bit (visited_control_parents, bb->index);\n}\n\n\n/* Find obviously necessary statements.  These are things like most function\n   calls, and stores to file level variables.\n\n   If EL is NULL, control statements are conservatively marked as\n   necessary.  Otherwise it contains the list of edges used by control\n   dependence analysis.  */\n\nstatic void\nfind_obviously_necessary_stmts (bool aggressive)\n{\n  basic_block bb;\n  gimple_stmt_iterator gsi;\n  edge e;\n  gimple *phi, *stmt;\n  int flags;\n\n  FOR_EACH_BB_FN (bb, cfun)\n    {\n      /* PHI nodes are never inherently necessary.  */\n      for (gsi = gsi_start_phis (bb); !gsi_end_p (gsi); gsi_next (&gsi))\n\t{\n\t  phi = gsi_stmt (gsi);\n\t  gimple_set_plf (phi, STMT_NECESSARY, false);\n\t}\n\n      /* Check all statements in the block.  */\n      for (gsi = gsi_start_bb (bb); !gsi_end_p (gsi); gsi_next (&gsi))\n\t{\n\t  stmt = gsi_stmt (gsi);\n\t  gimple_set_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY, false);\n\t  mark_stmt_if_obviously_necessary (stmt, aggressive);\n\t}\n    }\n\n  /* Pure and const functions are finite and thus have no infinite loops in\n     them.  */\n  flags = flags_from_decl_or_type (current_function_decl);\n  if ((flags & (ECF_CONST|ECF_PURE)) && !(flags & ECF_LOOPING_CONST_OR_PURE))\n    return;\n\n  /* Prevent the empty possibly infinite loops from being removed.  This is\n     needed to make the logic in remove_dead_stmt work to identify the\n     correct edge to keep when removing a controlling condition.  */\n  if (aggressive)\n    {\n      if (mark_irreducible_loops ())\n\tFOR_EACH_BB_FN (bb, cfun)\n\t  {\n\t    edge_iterator ei;\n\t    FOR_EACH_EDGE (e, ei, bb->succs)\n\t      if ((e->flags & EDGE_DFS_BACK)\n\t\t  && (e->flags & EDGE_IRREDUCIBLE_LOOP))\n\t\t{\n\t          if (dump_file)\n\t\t    fprintf (dump_file, \"Marking back edge of irreducible \"\n\t\t\t     \"loop %i->%i\\n\", e->src->index, e->dest->index);\n\t\t  mark_control_dependent_edges_necessary (e->dest, false);\n\t\t}\n\t  }\n\n      for (auto loop : loops_list (cfun, 0))\n\t/* For loops without an exit do not mark any condition.  */\n\tif (loop->exits->next->e && !finite_loop_p (loop))\n\t  {\n\t    if (dump_file)\n\t      fprintf (dump_file, \"cannot prove finiteness of loop %i\\n\",\n\t\t       loop->num);\n\t    mark_control_dependent_edges_necessary (loop->latch, false);\n\t  }\n    }\n}\n\n\n/* Return true if REF is based on an aliased base, otherwise false.  */\n\nstatic bool\nref_may_be_aliased (tree ref)\n{\n  if (TREE_CODE (ref) == WITH_SIZE_EXPR)\n    ref = TREE_OPERAND (ref, 0);\n  while (handled_component_p (ref))\n    ref = TREE_OPERAND (ref, 0);\n  if ((TREE_CODE (ref) == MEM_REF || TREE_CODE (ref) == TARGET_MEM_REF)\n      && TREE_CODE (TREE_OPERAND (ref, 0)) == ADDR_EXPR)\n    ref = TREE_OPERAND (TREE_OPERAND (ref, 0), 0);\n  return !(DECL_P (ref)\n\t   && !may_be_aliased (ref));\n}\n\nstatic bitmap visited = NULL;\nstatic unsigned int longest_chain = 0;\nstatic unsigned int total_chain = 0;\nstatic unsigned int nr_walks = 0;\nstatic bool chain_ovfl = false;\n\n/* Worker for the walker that marks reaching definitions of REF,\n   which is based on a non-aliased decl, necessary.  It returns\n   true whenever the defining statement of the current VDEF is\n   a kill for REF, as no dominating may-defs are necessary for REF\n   anymore.  DATA points to the basic-block that contains the\n   stmt that refers to REF.  */\n\nstatic bool\nmark_aliased_reaching_defs_necessary_1 (ao_ref *ref, tree vdef, void *data)\n{\n  gimple *def_stmt = SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (vdef);\n\n  /* All stmts we visit are necessary.  */\n  if (! gimple_clobber_p (def_stmt))\n    mark_operand_necessary (vdef);\n\n  /* If the stmt lhs kills ref, then we can stop walking.  */\n  if (gimple_has_lhs (def_stmt)\n      && TREE_CODE (gimple_get_lhs (def_stmt)) != SSA_NAME\n      /* The assignment is not necessarily carried out if it can throw\n         and we can catch it in the current function where we could inspect\n\t the previous value.\n         ??? For aggregate\n\t assignments or similar calls and non-call exceptions the LHS\n\t might throw as well.  */\n      && !stmt_can_throw_internal (cfun, def_stmt))\n    {\n      tree base, lhs = &reverse);\n      /* We can get MEM[symbol: sZ, index: D.8862_1] here,\n\t so base == refd->base does not always hold.  */\n      if (base == ref->base)\n\t{\n\t  /* For a must-alias check we need to need to be exactly the same.  */\n\t  else if (ref->ref\n\t\t   /* Make sure there is no induction variable involved\n\t\t      in the references (gcc.c-torture/execute/pr42142.c).\n\t\t      The simplest way is to check if the kill dominates\n\t\t      the use.  */\n\t\t   /* But when both are in the same block we cannot\n\t\t      easily tell whether we came from a backedge\n\t\t      unless we decide to compute stmt UIDs\n\t\t      (see PR58246).  */\n\t\t   && (basic_block) data != gimple_bb (def_stmt)\n\t\t   && dominated_by_p (CDI_DOMINATORS, (basic_block) data,\n\t\t\t\t      gimple_bb (def_stmt))\n\t\t   && operand_equal_p (ref->ref, lhs, 0))\n\t    return true;\n\t}\n    }\n\n  /* Otherwise keep walking.  */\n  return false;\n}\n\nstatic void\nmark_aliased_reaching_defs_necessary (gimple *stmt, tree ref)\n{\n  /* Should have been caught before calling this function.  */\n  gcc_checking_assert (!keep_all_vdefs_p ());\n\n  unsigned int chain;\n  ao_ref refd;\n  gcc_assert (!chain_ovfl);\n  ao_ref_init (&refd, ref);\n  chain = walk_aliased_vdefs (&refd, gimple_vuse (stmt),\n\t\t\t      mark_aliased_reaching_defs_necessary_1,\n\t\t\t      gimple_bb (stmt), NULL);\n  if (chain > longest_chain)\n    longest_chain = chain;\n  total_chain += chain;\n  nr_walks++;\n}\n\n/* Worker for the walker that marks reaching definitions of REF, which\n   is not based on a non-aliased decl.  For simplicity we need to end\n   up marking all may-defs necessary that are not based on a non-aliased\n   decl.  The only job of this walker is to skip may-defs based on\n   a non-aliased decl.  */\n\nstatic bool\nmark_all_reaching_defs_necessary_1 (ao_ref *ref ATTRIBUTE_UNUSED,\n\t\t\t\t    tree vdef, void *data ATTRIBUTE_UNUSED)\n{\n  gimple *def_stmt = SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (vdef);\n\n  /* We have to skip already visited (and thus necessary) statements\n     to make the chaining work after we dropped back to simple mode.  */\n  if (chain_ovfl\n      && bitmap_bit_p (processed, SSA_NAME_VERSION (vdef)))\n    {\n      gcc_assert (gimple_nop_p (def_stmt)\n\t\t  || gimple_plf (def_stmt, STMT_NECESSARY));\n      return false;\n    }\n\n  /* We want to skip stores to non-aliased variables.  */\n  if (!chain_ovfl\n      && gimple_assign_single_p (def_stmt))\n    {\n      tree lhs = gimple_assign_lhs (def_stmt);\n      if (!ref_may_be_aliased (lhs))\n\treturn false;\n    }\n\n  /* We want to skip statments that do not constitute stores but have\n     a virtual definition.  */\n  if (gcall *call = dyn_cast <gcall *> (def_stmt))\n    {\n      tree callee = gimple_call_fndecl (call);\n      if (callee != NULL_TREE\n\t  && fndecl_built_in_p (callee, BUILT_IN_NORMAL))\n\tswitch (DECL_FUNCTION_CODE (callee))\n\t  {\n\t  case BUILT_IN_MALLOC:\n\t  case BUILT_IN_ALIGNED_ALLOC:\n\t  case BUILT_IN_CALLOC:\n\t  CASE_BUILT_IN_ALLOCA:\n\t  case BUILT_IN_STRDUP:\n\t  case BUILT_IN_STRNDUP:\n\t  case BUILT_IN_FREE:\n\t  case BUILT_IN_GOMP_ALLOC:\n\t  case BUILT_IN_GOMP_FREE:\n\t    return false;\n\n\t  default:;\n\t  }\n\n      if (callee != NULL_TREE\n\t  && (DECL_IS_REPLACEABLE_OPERATOR_NEW_P (callee)\n\t      || DECL_IS_OPERATOR_DELETE_P (callee))\n\t  && gimple_call_from_new_or_delete (call))\n\treturn false;\n      if (is_removable_cxa_atexit_call (call))\n\treturn false;\n    }\n\n  if (! gimple_clobber_p (def_stmt))\n    mark_operand_necessary (vdef);\n\n  return false;\n}\n\nstatic void\nmark_all_reaching_defs_necessary (gimple *stmt)\n{\n  /* Should have been caught before calling this function.  */\n  gcc_checking_assert (!keep_all_vdefs_p ());\n  walk_aliased_vdefs (NULL, gimple_vuse (stmt),\n\t\t      mark_all_reaching_defs_necessary_1, NULL, &visited);\n}\n\n/* Return true for PHI nodes with one or identical arguments\n   can be removed.  */\nstatic bool\ndegenerate_phi_p (gimple *phi)\n{\n  unsigned int i;\n  tree op = gimple_phi_arg_def (phi, 0);\n  for (i = 1; i < gimple_phi_num_args (phi); i++)\n    if (gimple_phi_arg_def (phi, i) != op)\n      return false;\n  return true;\n}\n\n/* Return that NEW_CALL and DELETE_CALL are a valid pair of new\n   and delete  operators.  */\n\nstatic bool\nvalid_new_delete_pair_p (gimple *new_call, gimple *delete_call)\n{\n  tree new_asm = DECL_ASSEMBLER_NAME (gimple_call_fndecl (new_call));\n  tree delete_asm = DECL_ASSEMBLER_NAME (gimple_call_fndecl (delete_call));\n  return valid_new_delete_pair_p (new_asm, delete_asm);\n}\n\n/* Propagate necessity using the operands of necessary statements.\n   Process the uses on each statement in the worklist, and add all\n   feeding statements which contribute to the calculation of this\n   value to the worklist.\n\n   In conservative mode, EL is NULL.  */\n\nstatic void\npropagate_necessity (bool aggressive)\n{\n  gimple *stmt;\n\n  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n    fprintf (dump_file, \"\\nProcessing worklist:\\n\");\n\n  while (worklist.length () > 0)\n    {\n      /* Take STMT from worklist.  */\n      stmt = worklist.pop ();\n\n      if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n\t{\n\t  fprintf (dump_file, \"processing: \");\n\t  print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, stmt, 0, TDF_SLIM);\n\t  fprintf (dump_file, \"\\n\");\n\t}\n\n      if (aggressive)\n\t{\n\t  /* Mark the last statement of the basic blocks on which the block\n\t     containing STMT is control dependent, but only if we haven't\n\t     already done so.  */\n\t  basic_block bb = gimple_bb (stmt);\n\t  if (bb != ENTRY_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun)\n\t      && !bitmap_bit_p (visited_control_parents, bb->index))\n\t    mark_control_dependent_edges_necessary (bb, false);\n\t}\n\n      if (gimple_code (stmt) == GIMPLE_PHI\n\t  /* We do not process virtual PHI nodes nor do we track their\n\t     necessity.  */\n\t  && !virtual_operand_p (gimple_phi_result (stmt)))\n\t{\n\t  /* PHI nodes are somewhat special in that each PHI alternative has\n\t     data and control dependencies.  All the statements feeding the\n\t     PHI node's arguments are always necessary.  In aggressive mode,\n\t     we also consider the control dependent edges leading to the\n\t     predecessor block associated with each PHI alternative as\n\t     necessary.  */\n\t  gphi *phi = as_a <gphi *> (stmt);\n\t  size_t k;\n\n\t  for (k = 0; k < gimple_phi_num_args (stmt); k++)\n            {\n\t      tree arg = PHI_ARG_DEF (stmt, k);\n\t      if (TREE_CODE (arg) == SSA_NAME)\n\t\tmark_operand_necessary (arg);\n\t    }\n\n\t  /* For PHI operands it matters from where the control flow arrives\n\t     to the BB.  Consider the following example:\n\n\t     a=exp1;\n\t     b=exp2;\n\t     if (test)\n\t\t;\n\t     else\n\t\t;\n\t     c=PHI(a,b)\n\n\t     We need to mark control dependence of the empty basic blocks, since they\n\t     contains computation of PHI operands.\n\n\t     Doing so is too restrictive in the case the predecestor block is in\n\t     the loop. Consider:\n\n\t      if (b)\n\t\t{\n\t\t  int i;\n\t\t  for (i = 0; i<1000; ++i)\n\t\t    ;\n\t\t  j = 0;\n\t\t}\n\t      return j;\n\n\t     There is PHI for J in the BB containing return statement.\n\t     In this case the control dependence of predecestor block (that is\n\t     within the empty loop) also contains the block determining number\n\t     of iterations of the block that would prevent removing of empty\n\t     loop in this case.\n\n\t     This scenario can be avoided by splitting critical edges.\n\t     To save the critical edge splitting pass we identify how the control\n\t     dependence would look like if the edge was split.\n\n\t     Consider the modified CFG created from current CFG by splitting\n\t     edge B->C.  In the postdominance tree of modified CFG, C' is\n\t     always child of C.  There are two cases how chlids of C' can look\n\t     like:\n\n\t\t1) C' is leaf\n\n\t\t   In this case the only basic block C' is control dependent on is B.\n\n\t\t2) C' has single child that is B\n\n\t\t   In this case control dependence of C' is same as control\n\t\t   dependence of B in original CFG except for block B itself.\n\t\t   (since C' postdominate B in modified CFG)\n\n\t     Now how to decide what case happens?  There are two basic options:\n\n\t\ta) C postdominate B.  Then C immediately postdominate B and\n\t\t   case 2 happens iff there is no other way from B to C except\n\t\t   the edge B->C.\n\n\t\t   There is other way from B to C iff there is succesor of B that\n\t\t   is not postdominated by B.  Testing this condition is somewhat\n\t\t   expensive, because we need to iterate all succesors of B.\n\t\t   We are safe to assume that this does not happen: we will mark B\n\t\t   as needed when processing the other path from B to C that is\n\t\t   conrol dependent on B and marking control dependencies of B\n\t\t   itself is harmless because they will be processed anyway after\n\t\t   processing control statement in B.\n\n\t\tb) C does not postdominate B.  Always case 1 happens since there is\n\t\t   path from C to exit that does not go through B and thus also C'.  */\n\n\t  if (aggressive && !degenerate_phi_p (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      for (k = 0; k < gimple_phi_num_args (stmt); k++)\n\t\t{\n\t\t  basic_block arg_bb = gimple_phi_arg_edge (phi, k)->src;\n\n\t\t  if (gimple_bb (stmt)\n\t\t      != get_immediate_dominator (CDI_POST_DOMINATORS, arg_bb))\n\t\t    {\n\t\t      if (!mark_last_stmt_necessary (arg_bb))\n\t\t\tmark_control_dependent_edges_necessary (arg_bb, false);\n\t\t    }\n\t\t  else if (arg_bb != ENTRY_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun)\n\t\t           && !bitmap_bit_p (visited_control_parents,\n\t\t\t\t\t arg_bb->index))\n\t\t    mark_control_dependent_edges_necessary (arg_bb, true);\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\t}\n      else\n\t{\n\t  /* Propagate through the operands.  Examine all the USE, VUSE and\n\t     VDEF operands in this statement.  Mark all the statements\n\t     which feed this statement's uses as necessary.  */\n\t  ssa_op_iter iter;\n\t  tree use;\n\n\t  /* If this is a call to free which is directly fed by an\n\t     allocation function do not mark that necessary through\n\t     processing the argument.  */\n\t  bool is_delete_operator\n\t    = (is_gimple_call (stmt)\n\t       && gimple_call_from_new_or_delete (as_a <gcall *> (stmt))\n\t       && gimple_call_operator_delete_p (as_a <gcall *> (stmt)));\n\t  if (is_delete_operator\n\t      || gimple_call_builtin_p (stmt, BUILT_IN_FREE)\n\t      || gimple_call_builtin_p (stmt, BUILT_IN_GOMP_FREE))\n\t    {\n\t      tree ptr = gimple_call_arg (stmt, 0);\n\t      gcall *def_stmt;\n\t      /* If the pointer we free is defined by an allocation\n\t\t function do not add the call to the worklist.  */\n\t      if (TREE_CODE (ptr) == SSA_NAME\n\t\t  && (def_stmt = dyn_cast <gcall *> (SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (ptr)))\n\t\t  && is_removable_allocation_p (def_stmt, false))\n\t\t{\n\t\t  if (is_delete_operator\n\t\t      && !valid_new_delete_pair_p (def_stmt, stmt))\n\t\t    mark_operand_necessary (gimple_call_arg (stmt, 0));\n\n\t\t  /* Delete operators can have alignment and (or) size\n\t\t     as next arguments.  When being a SSA_NAME, they\n\t\t     must be marked as necessary.  Similarly GOMP_free.  */\n\t\t  if (gimple_call_num_args (stmt) >= 2)\n\t\t    for (unsigned i = 1; i < gimple_call_num_args (stmt);\n\t\t\t i++)\n\t\t      {\n\t\t\ttree arg = gimple_call_arg (stmt, i);\n\t\t\tif (TREE_CODE (arg) == SSA_NAME)\n\t\t\t  mark_operand_necessary (arg);\n\t\t      }\n\n\t\t  continue;\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\n\t  if (checks_return_value_of_removable_allocation_p (stmt))\n\t    continue;\n\n\t  FOR_EACH_SSA_TREE_OPERAND (use, stmt, iter, SSA_OP_USE)\n\t    mark_operand_necessary (use);\n\n\t  use = gimple_vuse (stmt);\n\t  if (!use)\n\t    continue;\n\n\t  /* No need to search for vdefs if we intrinsicly keep them all.  */\n\t  if (keep_all_vdefs_p ())\n\t    continue;\n\n\t  /* If we dropped to simple mode make all immediately\n\t     reachable definitions necessary.  */\n\t  if (chain_ovfl)\n\t    {\n\t      mark_all_reaching_defs_necessary (stmt);\n\t      continue;\n\t    }\n\n\t  /* For statements that may load from memory (have a VUSE) we\n\t     have to mark all reaching (may-)definitions as necessary.\n\t     We partition this task into two cases:\n\t      1) explicit loads based on decls that are not aliased\n\t      2) implicit loads (like calls) and explicit loads not\n\t         based on decls that are not aliased (like indirect\n\t\t references or loads from globals)\n\t     For 1) we mark all reaching may-defs as necessary, stopping\n\t     at dominating kills.  For 2) we want to mark all dominating\n\t     references necessary, but non-aliased ones which we handle\n\t     in 1).  By keeping a global visited bitmap for references\n\t     we walk for 2) we avoid quadratic behavior for those.  */\n\n\t  if (gcall *call = dyn_cast <gcall *> (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      tree callee = gimple_call_fndecl (call);\n\t      unsigned i;\n\n\t      if (callee != NULL_TREE\n\t\t  && (DECL_IS_REPLACEABLE_OPERATOR_NEW_P (callee)\n\t\t      || DECL_IS_OPERATOR_DELETE_P (callee))\n\t\t  && gimple_call_from_new_or_delete (call))\n\t\tcontinue;\n\n\t      if (is_removable_cxa_atexit_call (call))\n\t\tcontinue;\n\n\t      bool all_refs = false;\n\t      /* Calls implicitly load from memory, their arguments\n\t         in addition may explicitly perform memory loads.  */\n\t      for (i = 0; i < gimple_call_num_args (call); ++i)\n\t\t{\n\t\t  tree arg = gimple_call_arg (call, i);\n\t\t  if (TREE_CODE (arg) == SSA_NAME\n\t\t      || is_gimple_min_invariant (arg))\n\t\t    continue;\n\t\t  if (TREE_CODE (arg) == WITH_SIZE_EXPR)\n\t\t    arg = TREE_OPERAND (arg, 0);\n\t\t  if (!ref_may_be_aliased (arg))\n\t\t    mark_aliased_reaching_defs_necessary (call, arg);\n\t\t  else\n\t\t    all_refs = true;\n\t\t}\n\n\t      if (!all_refs && ipa_modref_callee_reads_no_memory_p (call))\n\t\tcontinue;\n\t      mark_all_reaching_defs_necessary (call);\n\t    }\n\t  else if (gimple_assign_single_p (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      tree rhs;\n\t      /* If this is a load mark things necessary.  */\n\t      rhs = gimple_assign_rhs1 (stmt);\n\t      if (TREE_CODE (rhs) != SSA_NAME\n\t\t  && !is_gimple_min_invariant (rhs)\n\t\t  && TREE_CODE (rhs) != CONSTRUCTOR)\n\t\t{\n\t\t  if (!ref_may_be_aliased (rhs))\n\t\t    mark_aliased_reaching_defs_necessary (stmt, rhs);\n\t\t  else\n\t\t    mark_all_reaching_defs_necessary (stmt);\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\t  else if (greturn *return_stmt = dyn_cast <greturn *> (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      tree rhs = gimple_return_retval (return_stmt);\n\t      /* A return statement may perform a load.  */\n\t      if (rhs\n\t\t  && TREE_CODE (rhs) != SSA_NAME\n\t\t  && !is_gimple_min_invariant (rhs)\n\t\t  && TREE_CODE (rhs) != CONSTRUCTOR)\n\t\t{\n\t\t  if (!ref_may_be_aliased (rhs))\n\t\t    mark_aliased_reaching_defs_necessary (stmt, rhs);\n\t\t  else\n\t\t    mark_all_reaching_defs_necessary (stmt);\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\t  else if (gasm *asm_stmt = dyn_cast <gasm *> (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      unsigned i;\n\t      mark_all_reaching_defs_necessary (stmt);\n\t      /* Inputs may perform loads.  */\n\t      for (i = 0; i < gimple_asm_ninputs (asm_stmt); ++i)\n\t\t{\n\t\t  tree op = TREE_VALUE (gimple_asm_input_op (asm_stmt, i));\n\t\t  if (TREE_CODE (op) != SSA_NAME\n\t\t      && !is_gimple_min_invariant (op)\n\t\t      && TREE_CODE (op) != CONSTRUCTOR\n\t\t      && !ref_may_be_aliased (op))\n\t\t    mark_aliased_reaching_defs_necessary (stmt, op);\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\t  else if (gimple_code (stmt) == GIMPLE_TRANSACTION)\n\t    {\n\t      /* The beginning of a transaction is a memory barrier.  */\n\t      /* ??? If we were really cool, we'd only be a barrier\n\t\t for the memories touched within the transaction.  */\n\t      mark_all_reaching_defs_necessary (stmt);\n\t    }\n\t  else\n\t    gcc_unreachable ();\n\n\t  /* If we over-used our alias oracle budget drop to simple\n\t     mode.  The cost metric allows quadratic behavior\n\t     (number of uses times number of may-defs queries) up to\n\t     a constant maximal number of queries and after that falls back to\n\t     super-linear complexity.  */\n\t  if (/* Constant but quadratic for small functions.  */\n\t      total_chain > 128 * 128\n\t      /* Linear in the number of may-defs.  */\n\t      && total_chain > 32 * longest_chain\n\t      /* Linear in the number of uses.  */\n\t      && total_chain > nr_walks * 32)\n\t    {\n\t      chain_ovfl = true;\n\t      if (visited)\n\t\tbitmap_clear (visited);\n\t    }\n\t}\n    }\n}\n\n/* Remove dead PHI nodes from block BB.  */\n\nstatic bool\nremove_dead_phis (basic_block bb)\n{\n  bool something_changed = false;\n  gphi *phi;\n  gphi_iterator gsi;\n\n  for (gsi = gsi_start_phis (bb); !gsi_end_p (gsi);)\n    {\n      stats.total_phis++;\n      phi = gsi.phi ();\n\n      /* We do not track necessity of virtual PHI nodes.  Instead do\n         very simple dead PHI removal here.  */\n      if (virtual_operand_p (gimple_phi_result (phi)))\n\t{\n\t  /* Virtual PHI nodes with one or identical arguments\n\t     can be removed.  */\n\t  if (!loops_state_satisfies_p (LOOP_CLOSED_SSA)\n\t      && degenerate_phi_p (phi))\n\t    {\n\t      tree vdef = gimple_phi_result (phi);\n\t      tree vuse = gimple_phi_arg_def (phi, 0);\n\n\t      use_operand_p use_p;\n\t      imm_use_iterator iter;\n\t      gimple *use_stmt;\n\t      FOR_EACH_IMM_USE_STMT (use_stmt, iter, vdef)\n\t\tFOR_EACH_IMM_USE_ON_STMT (use_p, iter)\n\t\t  SET_USE (use_p, vuse);\n\t      if (SSA_NAME_OCCURS_IN_ABNORMAL_PHI (vdef)\n\t          && TREE_CODE (vuse) == SSA_NAME)\n\t\tSSA_NAME_OCCURS_IN_ABNORMAL_PHI (vuse) = 1;\n\t    }\n\t  else\n\t    gimple_set_plf (phi, STMT_NECESSARY, true);\n\t}\n\n      if (!gimple_plf (phi, STMT_NECESSARY))\n\t{\n\t  something_changed = true;\n\t  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n\t    {\n\t      fprintf (dump_file, \"Deleting : \");\n\t      print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, phi, 0, TDF_SLIM);\n\t      fprintf (dump_file, \"\\n\");\n\t    }\n\n\t  remove_phi_node (&gsi, true);\n\t  stats.removed_phis++;\n\t  continue;\n\t}\n\n      gsi_next (&gsi);\n    }\n  return something_changed;\n}\n\n\n/* Remove dead statement pointed to by iterator I.  Receives the basic block BB\n   containing I so that we don't have to look it up.  */\n\nstatic void\nremove_dead_stmt (gimple_stmt_iterator *i, basic_block bb,\n\t\t  vec<edge> &to_remove_edges)\n{\n  gimple *stmt = gsi_stmt (*i);\n\n  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n    {\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"Deleting : \");\n      print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, stmt, 0, TDF_SLIM);\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"\\n\");\n    }\n\n  stats.removed++;\n\n  /* If we have determined that a conditional branch statement contributes\n     nothing to the program, then we not only remove it, but we need to update\n     the CFG.  We can chose any of edges out of BB as long as we are sure to not\n     close infinite loops.  This is done by always choosing the edge closer to\n     exit in inverted_rev_post_order_compute order.  */\n  if (is_ctrl_stmt (stmt))\n    {\n      edge_iterator ei;\n      edge e = NULL, e2;\n\n      /* See if there is only one non-abnormal edge.  */\n      if (single_succ_p (bb))\n        e = single_succ_edge (bb);\n      /* Otherwise chose one that is closer to bb with live statement in it.\n         To be able to chose one, we compute inverted post order starting from\n\t all BBs with live statements.  */\n      if (!e)\n\t{\n\t  if (!bb_postorder)\n\t    {\n\t      int *rpo = XNEWVEC (int, n_basic_blocks_for_fn (cfun));\n\t      int n = inverted_rev_post_order_compute (cfun, rpo,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t       &bb_contains_live_stmts);\n\t      bb_postorder = XNEWVEC (int, last_basic_block_for_fn (cfun));\n\t      for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i)\n\t\t bb_postorder[rpo[i]] = i;\n\t      free (rpo);\n\t    }\n          FOR_EACH_EDGE (e2, ei, bb->succs)\n\t    if (!e || e2->dest == EXIT_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun)\n\t\t|| bb_postorder [e->dest->index]\n\t\t   >= bb_postorder [e2->dest->index])\n\t      e = e2;\n\t}\n      gcc_assert (e);\n      e->probability = profile_probability::always ();\n\n      /* The edge is no longer associated with a conditional, so it does\n\t not have TRUE/FALSE flags.\n\t We are also safe to drop EH/ABNORMAL flags and turn them into\n\t normal control flow, because we know that all the destinations (including\n\t those odd edges) are equivalent for program execution.  */\n      e->flags &= ~(EDGE_TRUE_VALUE | EDGE_FALSE_VALUE | EDGE_EH | EDGE_ABNORMAL);\n\n      /* The lone outgoing edge from BB will be a fallthru edge.  */\n      e->flags |= EDGE_FALLTHRU;\n\n      /* Remove the remaining outgoing edges.  */\n      FOR_EACH_EDGE (e2, ei, bb->succs)\n\tif (e != e2)\n\t  {\n\t    /* If we made a BB unconditionally exit a loop or removed\n\t       an entry into an irreducible region, then this transform\n\t       alters the set of BBs in the loop.  Schedule a fixup.  */\n\t    if (loop_exit_edge_p (bb->loop_father, e)\n\t\t|| (e2->dest->flags & BB_IRREDUCIBLE_LOOP))\n\t      loops_state_set (LOOPS_NEED_FIXUP);\n\t    to_remove_edges.safe_push (e2);\n\t  }\n    }\n\n  /* If this is a store into a variable that is being optimized away,\n     add a debug bind stmt if possible.  */\n  if (MAY_HAVE_DEBUG_BIND_STMTS\n      && gimple_assign_single_p (stmt)\n      && is_gimple_val (gimple_assign_rhs1 (stmt)))\n    {\n      tree lhs = gimple_assign_lhs (stmt);\n      if ((VAR_P (lhs) || TREE_CODE (lhs) == PARM_DECL)\n\t  && !DECL_IGNORED_P (lhs)\n\t  && is_gimple_reg_type (TREE_TYPE (lhs))\n\t  && !is_global_var (lhs)\n\t  && !DECL_HAS_VALUE_EXPR_P (lhs))\n\t{\n\t  tree rhs = gimple_assign_rhs1 (stmt);\n\t  gdebug *note\n\t    = gimple_build_debug_bind (lhs, unshare_expr (rhs), stmt);\n\t  gsi_insert_after (i, note, GSI_SAME_STMT);\n\t}\n    }\n\n  unlink_stmt_vdef (stmt);\n  gsi_remove (i, true);\n  release_defs (stmt);\n}\n\n/* Helper for maybe_optimize_arith_overflow.  Find in *TP if there are any\n   uses of data (SSA_NAME) other than REALPART_EXPR referencing it.  */\n\nstatic tree\nfind_non_realpart_uses (tree *tp, int *walk_subtrees, void *data)\n{\n  if (TYPE_P (*tp) || TREE_CODE (*tp) == REALPART_EXPR)\n    *walk_subtrees = 0;\n  if (*tp == (tree) data)\n    return *tp;\n  return NULL_TREE;\n}\n\n/* If the IMAGPART_EXPR of the {ADD,SUB,MUL}_OVERFLOW result is never used,\n   but REALPART_EXPR is, optimize the {ADD,SUB,MUL}_OVERFLOW internal calls\n   into plain unsigned {PLUS,MINUS,MULT}_EXPR, and if needed reset debug\n   uses.  */\n\nstatic void\nmaybe_optimize_arith_overflow (gimple_stmt_iterator *gsi,\n\t\t\t       enum tree_code subcode)\n{\n  gimple *stmt = gsi_stmt (*gsi);\n  tree lhs = gimple_call_lhs (stmt);\n\n  if (lhs == NULL || TREE_CODE (lhs) != SSA_NAME)\n    return;\n\n  imm_use_iterator imm_iter;\n  use_operand_p use_p;\n  bool has_debug_uses = false;\n  bool has_realpart_uses = false;\n  bool has_other_uses = false;\n  FOR_EACH_IMM_USE_FAST (use_p, imm_iter, lhs)\n    {\n      gimple *use_stmt = USE_STMT (use_p);\n      if (is_gimple_debug (use_stmt))\n\thas_debug_uses = true;\n      else if (is_gimple_assign (use_stmt)\n\t       && gimple_assign_rhs_code (use_stmt) == REALPART_EXPR\n\t       && TREE_OPERAND (gimple_assign_rhs1 (use_stmt), 0) == lhs)\n\thas_realpart_uses = true;\n      else\n\t{\n\t  has_other_uses = true;\n\t  break;\n\t}\n    }\n\n  if (!has_realpart_uses || has_other_uses)\n    return;\n\n  tree arg0 = gimple_call_arg (stmt, 0);\n  tree arg1 = gimple_call_arg (stmt, 1);\n  location_t loc = gimple_location (stmt);\n  tree type = TREE_TYPE (TREE_TYPE (lhs));\n  tree utype = unsigned_type_for (type);\n  tree result = fold_build2_loc (loc, subcode, utype,\n\t\t\t\t fold_convert_loc (loc, utype, arg0),\n\t\t\t\t fold_convert_loc (loc, utype, arg1));\n  result = fold_convert_loc (loc, type, result);\n\n  if (has_debug_uses)\n    {\n      gimple *use_stmt;\n      FOR_EACH_IMM_USE_STMT (use_stmt, imm_iter, lhs)\n\t{\n\t  if (!gimple_debug_bind_p (use_stmt))\n\t    continue;\n\t  tree v = gimple_debug_bind_get_value (use_stmt);\n\t  if (walk_tree (&v, find_non_realpart_uses, lhs, NULL))\n\t    {\n\t      gimple_debug_bind_reset_value (use_stmt);\n\t      update_stmt (use_stmt);\n\t    }\n\t}\n    }\n\n  if (TREE_CODE (result) == INTEGER_CST && TREE_OVERFLOW (result))\n    result = drop_tree_overflow (result);\n  tree overflow = build_zero_cst (type);\n  tree ctype = build_complex_type (type);\n  if (TREE_CODE (result) == INTEGER_CST)\n    result = build_complex (ctype, result, overflow);\n  else\n    result = build2_loc (gimple_location (stmt), COMPLEX_EXPR,\n\t\t\t ctype, result, overflow);\n\n  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n    {\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"Transforming call: \");\n      print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, stmt, 0, TDF_SLIM);\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"because the overflow result is never used into: \");\n      print_generic_stmt (dump_file, result, TDF_SLIM);\n      fprintf (dump_file, \"\\n\");\n    }\n\n  gimplify_and_update_call_from_tree (gsi, result);\n}\n\n/* Returns whether the control parents of BB are preserved.  */\n\nstatic bool\ncontrol_parents_preserved_p (basic_block bb)\n{\n  /* If we marked the control parents from BB they are preserved.  */\n  if (bitmap_bit_p (visited_control_parents, bb->index))\n    return true;\n\n  /* But they can also end up being marked from elsewhere.  */\n  bitmap_iterator bi;\n  unsigned edge_number;\n  EXECUTE_IF_SET_IN_BITMAP (cd->get_edges_dependent_on (bb->index),\n\t\t\t    0, edge_number, bi)\n    {\n      basic_block cd_bb = cd->get_edge_src (edge_number);\n      if (cd_bb != bb\n\t  && !bitmap_bit_p (last_stmt_necessary, cd_bb->index))\n\treturn false;\n    }\n  /* And cache the result.  */\n  bitmap_set_bit (visited_control_parents, bb->index);\n  return true;\n}\n\n/* If basic block is empty, we can remove conditionals that controls\n   its execution.  However in some cases the empty BB can stay live\n   (such as when it was a header of empty loop).  In this case we\n   need to update its count.  Since regions of dead BBs are acyclic\n   we simply propagate counts forward from live BBs to dead ones.  */\n\nstatic void\npropagate_counts ()\n{\n  basic_block bb;\n  auto_vec<basic_block, 16> queue;\n  hash_map <basic_block, int> cnt;\n\n  FOR_EACH_BB_FN (bb, cfun)\n    if (!bitmap_bit_p (bb_contains_live_stmts, bb->index))\n      {\n\tint n = 0;\n\tfor (edge e : bb->preds)\n\t  if (e->src != ENTRY_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun)\n\t      && !bitmap_bit_p (bb_contains_live_stmts, e->src->index))\n\t    n++;\n\tif (!n)\n\t  queue.safe_push (bb);\n\tcnt.put (bb, n);\n      }\n  while (!queue.is_empty ())\n    {\n      basic_block bb = queue.pop ();\n      profile_count sum = profile_count::zero ();\n\n      for (edge e : bb->preds)\n\t{\n\t  sum += e->count ();\n\t  gcc_checking_assert (!cnt.get (e->src));\n\t}\n      /* If we have partial profile and some counts of incomming edges are\n\t unknown, it is probably better to keep the existing count.\n\t We could also propagate bi-directionally.  */\n      if (sum.initialized_p () && !(sum == bb->count))\n\t{\n\t  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n\t    {\n\t      fprintf (dump_file, \"Updating count of empty bb %i from \",\n\t\t       bb->index);\n\t      bb->count.dump (dump_file);\n\t      fprintf (dump_file, \" to \");\n\t      sum.dump (dump_file);\n\t      fprintf (dump_file, \"\\n\");\n\t    }\n\t  bb->count = sum;\n\t}\n      cnt.remove (bb);\n      for (edge e : bb->succs)\n\tif (int *n = cnt.get (e->dest))\n\t  {\n\t    (*n)--;\n\t    if (!*n)\n\t      queue.safe_push (e->dest);\n\t  }\n    }\n  /* Do not check that all blocks has been processed, since for\n     empty infinite loops this is not the case.  */\n}\n\n/* Eliminate unnecessary statements. Any instruction not marked as necessary\n   contributes nothing to the program, and can be deleted.  */\n\nstatic bool\neliminate_unnecessary_stmts (bool aggressive)\n{\n  bool something_changed = false;\n  basic_block bb;\n  gimple_stmt_iterator gsi, psi;\n  gimple *stmt;\n  auto_vec<edge> to_remove_edges;\n\n  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n    fprintf (dump_file, \"\\nEliminating unnecessary statements:\\n\");\n\n  bool had_setjmp = cfun->calls_setjmp;\n  clear_special_calls ();\n\n  /* Walking basic blocks and statements in reverse order avoids\n     releasing SSA names before any other DEFs that refer to them are\n     released.  This helps avoid loss of debug information, as we get\n     a chance to propagate all RHSs of removed SSAs into debug uses,\n     rather than only the latest ones.  E.g., consider:\n\n     x_3 = y_1 + z_2;\n     a_5 = x_3 - b_4;\n     # DEBUG a => a_5\n\n     If we were to release x_3 before a_5, when we reached a_5 and\n     tried to substitute it into the debug stmt, we'd see x_3 there,\n     but x_3's DEF, type, etc would have already been disconnected.\n     By going backwards, the debug stmt first changes to:\n\n     # DEBUG a => x_3 - b_4\n\n     and then to:\n\n     # DEBUG a => y_1 + z_2 - b_4\n\n     as desired.  */\n  gcc_assert (dom_info_available_p (CDI_DOMINATORS));\n  auto_vec<basic_block> h;\n  h = get_all_dominated_blocks (CDI_DOMINATORS,\n\t\t\t\tsingle_succ (ENTRY_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun)));\n\n  while (h.length ())\n    {\n      bb = h.pop ();\n\n      /* Remove dead statements.  */\n      auto_bitmap debug_seen;\n      hash_set<int_hash <location_t, 0>> locs_seen;\n      for (gsi = gsi_last_bb (bb); !gsi_end_p (gsi); gsi = psi)\n\t{\n\t  stmt = gsi_stmt (gsi);\n\n\t  psi = gsi;\n\t  gsi_prev (&psi);\n\n\t  stats.total++;\n\n\t  /* We can mark a call to free as not necessary if the\n\t     defining statement of its argument is not necessary\n\t     (and thus is getting removed).  */\n\t  if (gimple_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY)\n\t      && (gimple_call_builtin_p (stmt, BUILT_IN_FREE)\n\t\t  || (is_gimple_call (stmt)\n\t\t      && gimple_call_from_new_or_delete (as_a <gcall *> (stmt))\n\t\t      && gimple_call_operator_delete_p (as_a <gcall *> (stmt)))))\n\t    {\n\t      tree ptr = gimple_call_arg (stmt, 0);\n\t      if (TREE_CODE (ptr) == SSA_NAME)\n\t\t{\n\t\t  gimple *def_stmt = SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (ptr);\n\t\t  if (!gimple_nop_p (def_stmt)\n\t\t      && !gimple_plf (def_stmt, STMT_NECESSARY))\n\t\t    gimple_set_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY, false);\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\t  /* Conditional checking that return value of allocation is non-NULL\n\t     can be turned to constant if the allocation itself\n\t     is unnecesary.  */\n\t  if (gimple_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY)\n\t      && gimple_code (stmt) == GIMPLE_COND\n\t      && TREE_CODE (gimple_cond_lhs (stmt)) == SSA_NAME)\n\t    {\n\t      gimple *def_stmt = SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (gimple_cond_lhs (stmt));\n\t      if (!gimple_nop_p (def_stmt)\n\t\t  && !gimple_plf (def_stmt, STMT_NECESSARY))\n\t\t{\n\t\t  gcc_checking_assert\n\t\t\t(checks_return_value_of_removable_allocation_p (stmt));\n\t\t  gimple_cond_set_lhs (as_a <gcond *>(stmt),\n\t\t\t\t       build_one_cst\n\t\t\t\t\t (TREE_TYPE (gimple_cond_rhs (stmt))));\n\t\t  update_stmt (stmt);\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\n\t  /* If GSI is not necessary then remove it.  */\n\t  if (!gimple_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY))\n\t    {\n\t      /* Keep clobbers that we can keep live live.  */\n\t      if (gimple_clobber_p (stmt))\n\t\t{\n\t\t  ssa_op_iter iter;\n\t\t  use_operand_p use_p;\n\t\t  bool dead = false;\n\t\t  FOR_EACH_SSA_USE_OPERAND (use_p, stmt, iter, SSA_OP_USE)\n\t\t    {\n\t\t      tree name = USE_FROM_PTR (use_p);\n\t\t      if (!SSA_NAME_IS_DEFAULT_DEF (name)\n\t\t\t  && !bitmap_bit_p (processed, SSA_NAME_VERSION (name)))\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t  dead = true;\n\t\t\t  break;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t    }\n\t\t  if (!dead\n\t\t      /* When doing CD-DCE we have to ensure all controls\n\t\t\t of the stmt are still live.  */\n\t\t      && (!aggressive || control_parents_preserved_p (bb)))\n\t\t    {\n\t\t      bitmap_clear (debug_seen);\n\t\t      continue;\n\t\t    }\n\t\t}\n\t      if (!is_gimple_debug (stmt))\n\t\tsomething_changed = true;\n\t      remove_dead_stmt (&gsi, bb, to_remove_edges);\n\t      continue;\n\t    }\n\t  else if (gcall *call_stmt = dyn_cast <gcall *> (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      tree name = gimple_call_lhs (call_stmt);\n\n\t      notice_special_calls (call_stmt);\n\n\t      /* When LHS of var = call (); is dead, simplify it into\n\t\t call (); saving one operand.  */\n\t      if (name\n\t\t  && TREE_CODE (name) == SSA_NAME\n\t\t  && !bitmap_bit_p (processed, SSA_NAME_VERSION (name))\n\t\t  /* Avoid doing so for allocation calls which we\n\t\t     did not mark as necessary, it will confuse the\n\t\t     special logic we apply to malloc/free pair removal.  */\n\t\t  && !is_removable_allocation_p (call_stmt, false))\n\t\t{\n\t\t  something_changed = true;\n\t\t  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n\t\t    {\n\t\t      fprintf (dump_file, \"Deleting LHS of call: \");\n\t\t      print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, call_stmt, 0, TDF_SLIM);\n\t\t      fprintf (dump_file, \"\\n\");\n\t\t    }\n\n\t\t  gimple_call_set_lhs (call_stmt, NULL_TREE);\n\t\t  maybe_clean_or_replace_eh_stmt (call_stmt, call_stmt);\n\t\t  update_stmt (call_stmt);\n\t\t  release_ssa_name (name);\n\n\t\t  /* __builtin_stack_save without lhs is not needed.  */\n\t\t  if (gimple_call_builtin_p (call_stmt, BUILT_IN_STACK_SAVE))\n\t\t    remove_dead_stmt (&gsi, bb, to_remove_edges);\n\t\t  /* GOMP_SIMD_LANE (unless three argument) or ASAN_POISON\n\t\t     without lhs is not needed.  */\n\t\t  else if (gimple_call_internal_p (call_stmt))\n\t\t    switch (gimple_call_internal_fn (call_stmt))\n\t\t      {\n\t\t      case IFN_GOMP_SIMD_LANE:\n\t\t\tif (gimple_call_num_args (call_stmt) >= 3\n\t\t\t    && !integer_nonzerop\n\t\t\t\t\t(gimple_call_arg (call_stmt, 2)))\n\t\t\t  break;\n\t\t\t/* FALLTHRU */\n\t\t      case IFN_ASAN_POISON:\n\t\t\tremove_dead_stmt (&gsi, bb, to_remove_edges);\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t      default:\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t      }\n\t\t}\n\t      else if (gimple_call_internal_p (call_stmt))\n\t\tswitch (gimple_call_internal_fn (call_stmt))\n\t\t  {\n\t\t  case IFN_ADD_OVERFLOW:\n\t\t    maybe_optimize_arith_overflow (&gsi, PLUS_EXPR);\n\t\t    break;\n\t\t  case IFN_SUB_OVERFLOW:\n\t\t    maybe_optimize_arith_overflow (&gsi, MINUS_EXPR);\n\t\t    break;\n\t\t  case IFN_MUL_OVERFLOW:\n\t\t    maybe_optimize_arith_overflow (&gsi, MULT_EXPR);\n\t\t    break;\n\t\t  case IFN_UADDC:\n\t\t    if (integer_zerop (gimple_call_arg (call_stmt, 2)))\n\t\t      maybe_optimize_arith_overflow (&gsi, PLUS_EXPR);\n\t\t    break;\n\t\t  case IFN_USUBC:\n\t\t    if (integer_zerop (gimple_call_arg (call_stmt, 2)))\n\t\t      maybe_optimize_arith_overflow (&gsi, MINUS_EXPR);\n\t\t    break;\n\t\t  default:\n\t\t    break;\n\t\t  }\n\t    }\n\t  else if (gimple_debug_bind_p (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      /* We are only keeping the last debug-bind of a\n\t         non-DEBUG_EXPR_DECL variable in a series of\n\t\t debug-bind stmts.  */\n\t      tree var = gimple_debug_bind_get_var (stmt);\n\t      if (TREE_CODE (var) != DEBUG_EXPR_DECL\n\t\t  && !bitmap_set_bit (debug_seen, DECL_UID (var)))\n\t\tremove_dead_stmt (&gsi, bb, to_remove_edges);\n\t      continue;\n\t    }\n\t  else if (gimple_debug_begin_stmt_p (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      /* We are only keeping the last debug-begin in a series of\n\t\t debug-begin stmts.  */\n\t      if (locs_seen.add (gimple_location (stmt)))\n\t\tremove_dead_stmt (&gsi, bb, to_remove_edges);\n\t      continue;\n\t    }\n\t  locs_seen.empty ();\n\t  bitmap_clear (debug_seen);\n\t}\n\n      /* Remove dead PHI nodes.  */\n      something_changed |= remove_dead_phis (bb);\n    }\n\n  /* First remove queued edges.  */\n  if (!to_remove_edges.is_empty ())\n    {\n      /* Remove edges.  We've delayed this to not get bogus debug stmts\n         during PHI node removal.  */\n      for (unsigned i = 0; i < to_remove_edges.length (); ++i)\n\tremove_edge (to_remove_edges[i]);\n      cfg_altered = true;\n    }\n  /* When we cleared calls_setjmp we can purge all abnormal edges.  Do so.\n     ???  We'd like to assert that setjmp calls do not pop out of nothing\n     but we currently lack a per-stmt way of noting whether a call was\n     recognized as returns-twice (or rather receives-control).  */\n  if (!cfun->calls_setjmp && had_setjmp)\n    {\n      /* Make sure we only remove the edges, not dominated blocks.  Using\n\t gimple_purge_dead_abnormal_call_edges would do that and we\n\t cannot free dominators yet.  */\n      FOR_EACH_BB_FN (bb, cfun)\n\tif (gcall *stmt = safe_dyn_cast <gcall *> (*gsi_last_bb (bb)))\n\t  if (!stmt_can_make_abnormal_goto (stmt))\n\t    {\n\t      edge_iterator ei;\n\t      edge e;\n\t      for (ei = ei_start (bb->succs); (e = ei_safe_edge (ei)); )\n\t\t{\n\t\t  if (e->flags & EDGE_ABNORMAL)\n\t\t    {\n\t\t      if (e->flags & EDGE_FALLTHRU)\n\t\t\te->flags &= ~EDGE_ABNORMAL;\n\t\t      else\n\t\t\tremove_edge (e);\n\t\t      cfg_altered = true;\n\t\t    }\n\t\t  else\n\t\t    ei_next (&ei);\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n    }\n\n  /* Now remove the unreachable blocks.  */\n  if (cfg_altered)\n    {\n      basic_block prev_bb;\n\n      find_unreachable_blocks ();\n\n      /* Delete all unreachable basic blocks in reverse dominator order.  */\n      for (bb = EXIT_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun)->prev_bb;\n\t   bb != ENTRY_BLOCK_PTR_FOR_FN (cfun); bb = prev_bb)\n\t{\n\t  prev_bb = bb->prev_bb;\n\n\t  if ((bb_contains_live_stmts\n\t       && !bitmap_bit_p (bb_contains_live_stmts, bb->index))\n\t      || !(bb->flags & BB_REACHABLE))\n\t    {\n\t      /* Since we don't track liveness of virtual PHI nodes, it is\n\t\t possible that we rendered some PHI nodes unreachable while\n\t\t they are still in use.  Mark them for renaming.  */\n\t      for (gphi_iterator gsi = gsi_start_phis (bb); !gsi_end_p (gsi);\n\t\t   gsi_next (&gsi))\n\t\tif (virtual_operand_p (gimple_phi_result (gsi.phi ())))\n\t\t  {\n\t\t    bool found = false;\n\t\t    imm_use_iterator iter;\n\n\t\t    FOR_EACH_IMM_USE_STMT (stmt, iter,\n\t\t\t\t\t   gimple_phi_result (gsi.phi ()))\n\t\t      {\n\t\t\tif (!(gimple_bb (stmt)->flags & BB_REACHABLE))\n\t\t\t  continue;\n\t\t\tif (gimple_code (stmt) == GIMPLE_PHI\n\t\t\t    || gimple_plf (stmt, STMT_NECESSARY))\n\t\t\t  {\n\t\t\t    found = true;\n\t\t\t    break;\n\t\t\t  }\n\t\t      }\n\t\t    if (found)\n\t\t      mark_virtual_phi_result_for_renaming (gsi.phi ());\n\t\t  }\n\n\t      if (!(bb->flags & BB_REACHABLE))\n\t\t{\n\t\t  /* Speed up the removal of blocks that don't\n\t\t     dominate others.  Walking backwards, this should\n\t\t     be the common case.  ??? Do we need to recompute\n\t\t     dominators because of cfg_altered?  */\n\t\t  if (!first_dom_son (CDI_DOMINATORS, bb))\n\t\t    delete_basic_block (bb);\n\t\t  else\n\t\t    {\n\t\t      h = get_all_dominated_blocks (CDI_DOMINATORS, bb);\n\n\t\t      while (h.length ())\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t  bb = h.pop ();\n\t\t\t  prev_bb = bb->prev_bb;\n\t\t\t  /* Rearrangements to the CFG may have failed\n\t\t\t     to update the dominators tree, so that\n\t\t\t     formerly-dominated blocks are now\n\t\t\t     otherwise reachable.  */\n\t\t\t  if (!!(bb->flags & BB_REACHABLE))\n\t\t\t    continue;\n\t\t\t  delete_basic_block (bb);\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t      h.release ();\n\t\t    }\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\t}\n      if (bb_contains_live_stmts)\n\tpropagate_counts ();\n    }\n\n  if (bb_postorder)\n    free (bb_postorder);\n  bb_postorder = NULL;\n\n  return something_changed;\n}\n\n\n/* Print out removed statement statistics.  */\n\nstatic void\nprint_stats (void)\n{\n  float percg;\n\n  percg = ((float) stats.removed / (float) stats.total) * 100;\n  fprintf (dump_file, \"Removed %d of %d statements (%d%%)\\n\",\n\t   stats.removed, stats.total, (int) percg);\n\n  if (stats.total_phis == 0)\n    percg = 0;\n  else\n    percg = ((float) stats.removed_phis / (float) stats.total_phis) * 100;\n\n  fprintf (dump_file, \"Removed %d of %d PHI nodes (%d%%)\\n\",\n\t   stats.removed_phis, stats.total_phis, (int) percg);\n}\n\n/* Initialization for this pass.  Set up the used data structures.  */\n\nstatic void\ntree_dce_init (bool aggressive)\n{\n  memset ((void *) &stats, 0, sizeof (stats));\n\n  if (aggressive)\n    {\n      last_stmt_necessary = sbitmap_alloc (last_basic_block_for_fn (cfun));\n      bitmap_clear (last_stmt_necessary);\n      bb_contains_live_stmts = sbitmap_alloc (last_basic_block_for_fn (cfun));\n      bitmap_clear (bb_contains_live_stmts);\n    }\n\n  processed = sbitmap_alloc (num_ssa_names + 1);\n  bitmap_clear (processed);\n\n  worklist.create (64);\n  cfg_altered = false;\n}\n\n/* Cleanup after this pass.  */\n\nstatic void\ntree_dce_done (bool aggressive)\n{\n  if (aggressive)\n    {\n      delete cd;\n      sbitmap_free (visited_control_parents);\n      sbitmap_free (last_stmt_necessary);\n      sbitmap_free (bb_contains_live_stmts);\n      bb_contains_live_stmts = NULL;\n    }\n\n  sbitmap_free (processed);\n\n  worklist.release ();\n}\n\n\n/* Main routine to eliminate dead code.\n\n   AGGRESSIVE controls the aggressiveness of the algorithm.\n   In conservative mode, we ignore control dependence and simply declare\n   all but the most trivially dead branches necessary.  This mode is fast.\n   In aggressive mode, control dependences are taken into account, which\n   results in more dead code elimination, but at the cost of some time.  */\n\nstatic unsigned int\nperform_tree_ssa_dce (bool aggressive)\n{\n  bool something_changed = 0;\n  unsigned todo = 0;\n\n  /* Preheaders are needed for SCEV to work.\n     Simple lateches and recorded exits improve chances that loop will\n     proved to be finite in testcases such as in loop-15.c and loop-24.c  */\n  bool in_loop_pipeline = scev_initialized_p ();\n  if (aggressive && ! in_loop_pipeline)\n    {\n      loop_optimizer_init (LOOPS_NORMAL\n\t\t\t   | LOOPS_HAVE_RECORDED_EXITS);\n      scev_initialize ();\n    }\n\n  if (aggressive && make_forwarders_with_degenerate_phis (cfun))\n    todo |= TODO_cleanup_cfg;\n\n  calculate_dominance_info (CDI_DOMINATORS);\n\n  tree_dce_init (aggressive);\n\n  if (aggressive)\n    {\n      /* Compute control dependence.  */\n      calculate_dominance_info (CDI_POST_DOMINATORS);\n      cd = new control_dependences ();\n\n      visited_control_parents =\n\tsbitmap_alloc (last_basic_block_for_fn (cfun));\n      bitmap_clear (visited_control_parents);\n\n      mark_dfs_back_edges ();\n    }\n\n  find_obviously_necessary_stmts (aggressive);\n\n  if (aggressive && ! in_loop_pipeline)\n    {\n      scev_finalize ();\n      loop_optimizer_finalize ();\n    }\n\n  longest_chain = 0;\n  total_chain = 0;\n  nr_walks = 0;\n  chain_ovfl = false;\n  visited = BITMAP_ALLOC (NULL);\n  propagate_necessity (aggressive);\n  BITMAP_FREE (visited);\n\n  something_changed |= eliminate_unnecessary_stmts (aggressive);\n  something_changed |= cfg_altered;\n\n  /* We do not update postdominators, so free them unconditionally.  */\n  free_dominance_info (CDI_POST_DOMINATORS);\n\n  /* If we removed paths in the CFG, then we need to update\n     dominators as well.  I haven't investigated the possibility\n     of incrementally updating dominators.  */\n  if (cfg_altered)\n    free_dominance_info (CDI_DOMINATORS);\n\n  statistics_counter_event (cfun, \"Statements deleted\", stats.removed);\n  statistics_counter_event (cfun, \"PHI nodes deleted\", stats.removed_phis);\n\n  /* Debugging dumps.  */\n  if (dump_file && (dump_flags & (TDF_STATS|TDF_DETAILS)))\n    print_stats ();\n\n  tree_dce_done (aggressive);\n\n  if (something_changed)\n    {\n      free_numbers_of_iterations_estimates (cfun);\n      if (in_loop_pipeline)\n\tscev_reset ();\n      todo |= TODO_update_ssa | TODO_cleanup_cfg;\n    }\n  return todo;\n}\n\nnamespace {\n\nconst pass_data pass_data_dce =\n{\n  GIMPLE_PASS, /* type */\n  \"dce\", /* name */\n  OPTGROUP_NONE, /* optinfo_flags */\n  TV_TREE_DCE, /* tv_id */\n  ( PROP_cfg | PROP_ssa ), /* properties_required */\n  0, /* properties_provided */\n  0, /* properties_destroyed */\n  0, /* todo_flags_start */\n  0, /* todo_flags_finish */\n};\n\nclass pass_dce_base : public gimple_opt_pass\n{\npublic:\n  /* opt_pass methods: */\n  bool gate (function *) final override { return flag_tree_dce != 0; }\n  void set_pass_param (unsigned n, bool param) final override\n    {\n      gcc_assert (n == 0 || n == 1);\n      if (n == 0)\n\tupdate_address_taken_p = param;\n      else if (n == 1)\n\tremove_unused_locals_p = param;\n    }\n\nprotected:\n  pass_dce_base (const pass_data &data, gcc::context *ctxt)\n    : gimple_opt_pass (data, ctxt)\n  {}\n  unsigned int execute_dce (function *, bool aggressive)\n    {\n      return (perform_tree_ssa_dce (aggressive)\n\t      | (remove_unused_locals_p ? TODO_remove_unused_locals : 0)\n\t      | (update_address_taken_p ? TODO_update_address_taken : 0));\n    }\n\nprivate:\n  bool update_address_taken_p = false;\n  bool remove_unused_locals_p = false;\n}; // class pass_dce_base\n\n\nclass pass_dce : public pass_dce_base\n{\npublic:\n  pass_dce (gcc::context *ctxt)\n    : pass_dce_base (pass_data_dce, ctxt)\n  {}\n\n  /* opt_pass methods: */\n  opt_pass * clone () final override { return new pass_dce (m_ctxt); }\n  unsigned int execute (function *func) final override\n    {\n      return execute_dce (func, /*aggressive=*/false);\n    }\n\n}; // class pass_dce\n\n} // anon namespace\n\ngimple_opt_pass *\nmake_pass_dce (gcc::context *ctxt)\n{\n  return new pass_dce (ctxt);\n}\n\nnamespace {\n\nconst pass_data pass_data_cd_dce =\n{\n  GIMPLE_PASS, /* type */\n  \"cddce\", /* name */\n  OPTGROUP_NONE, /* optinfo_flags */\n  TV_TREE_CD_DCE, /* tv_id */\n  ( PROP_cfg | PROP_ssa ), /* properties_required */\n  0, /* properties_provided */\n  0, /* properties_destroyed */\n  0, /* todo_flags_start */\n  0, /* todo_flags_finish */\n};\n\nclass pass_cd_dce : public pass_dce_base\n{\npublic:\n  pass_cd_dce (gcc::context *ctxt)\n    : pass_dce_base (pass_data_cd_dce, ctxt)\n  {}\n\n  /* opt_pass methods: */\n  opt_pass * clone () final override { return new pass_cd_dce (m_ctxt); }\n  unsigned int execute (function *func) final override\n    {\n      return execute_dce (func, /*aggressive=*/optimize >= 2);\n    }\n\n}; // class pass_cd_dce\n\n} // anon namespace\n\ngimple_opt_pass *\nmake_pass_cd_dce (gcc::context *ctxt)\n{\n  return new pass_cd_dce (ctxt);\n}\n\n\n/* A cheap DCE interface.  WORKLIST is a list of possibly dead stmts and\n   is consumed by this function.  The function has linear complexity in\n   the number of dead stmts with a constant factor like the average SSA\n   use operands number.  */\n\nvoid\nsimple_dce_from_worklist (bitmap worklist, bitmap need_eh_cleanup)\n{\n  int phiremoved = 0;\n  int stmtremoved = 0;\n  while (! bitmap_empty_p (worklist))\n    {\n      /* Pop item.  */\n      unsigned i = bitmap_clear_first_set_bit (worklist);\n\n      tree def = ssa_name (i);\n      /* Removed by somebody else or still in use.\n\t Note use in itself for a phi node is not counted as still in use.  */\n      if (!def)\n\tcontinue;\n      if (!has_zero_uses (def))\n\t{\n\t  gimple *def_stmt = SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (def);\n\n\t  if (gimple_code (def_stmt) != GIMPLE_PHI)\n\t    continue;\n\n\t  imm_use_iterator use_iter;\n\t  use_operand_p use_p;\n\t  bool canremove = true;\n\n\t  FOR_EACH_IMM_USE_FAST (use_p, use_iter, def)\n\t    {\n\t      gimple *use_stmt = USE_STMT (use_p);\n\t      /* Ignore debug statements. */\n\t      if (is_gimple_debug (use_stmt))\n\t\tcontinue;\n\t      if (use_stmt != def_stmt)\n\t\t{\n\t\t  canremove = false;\n\t\t  break;\n\t\t}\n\t    }\n\t  if (!canremove)\n\t    continue;\n\t}\n\n      gimple *t = SSA_NAME_DEF_STMT (def);\n      if (gimple_has_side_effects (t))\n\t{\n\t  if (gcall *call = dyn_cast <gcall *> (t))\n\t    {\n\t      gimple_call_set_lhs (call, NULL_TREE);\n\t      update_stmt (call);\n\t      release_ssa_name (def);\n\t    }\n\t  continue;\n\t}\n\n      /* The defining statement needs to be defining only this name.\n\t ASM is the only statement that can define more than one\n\t name. */\n      if (is_a<gasm *>(t)\n\t  && !single_ssa_def_operand (t, SSA_OP_ALL_DEFS))\n\tcontinue;\n\n      /* Don't remove statements that are needed for non-call\n\t eh to work.  */\n      if (stmt_unremovable_because_of_non_call_eh_p (cfun, t))\n\tcontinue;\n\n      /* Tell the caller that we removed a statement that might\n\t throw so it could cleanup the cfg for that block. */\n      if (need_eh_cleanup && stmt_could_throw_p (cfun, t))\n\tbitmap_set_bit (need_eh_cleanup, gimple_bb (t)->index);\n\n      /* Add uses to the worklist.  */\n      ssa_op_iter iter;\n      use_operand_p use_p;\n      FOR_EACH_PHI_OR_STMT_USE (use_p, t, iter, SSA_OP_USE)\n\t{\n\t  tree use = USE_FROM_PTR (use_p);\n\t  if (TREE_CODE (use) == SSA_NAME\n\t      && ! SSA_NAME_IS_DEFAULT_DEF (use))\n\t    bitmap_set_bit (worklist, SSA_NAME_VERSION (use));\n\t}\n\n      /* Remove stmt.  */\n      if (dump_file && (dump_flags & TDF_DETAILS))\n\t{\n\t  fprintf (dump_file, \"Removing dead stmt:\");\n\t  print_gimple_stmt (dump_file, t, 0);\n\t}\n      gimple_stmt_iterator gsi = gsi_for_stmt (t);\n      if (gimple_code (t) == GIMPLE_PHI)\n\t{\n\t  remove_phi_node (&gsi, true);\n\t  phiremoved++;\n\t}\n      else\n\t{\n\t  unlink_stmt_vdef (t);\n\t  gsi_remove (&gsi, true);\n\t  release_defs (t);\n\t  stmtremoved++;\n\t}\n    }\n  statistics_counter_event (cfun, \"PHIs removed\",\n\t\t\t    phiremoved);\n  statistics_counter_event (cfun, \"Statements removed\",\n\t\t\t    stmtremoved);\n}\n","numLines":2258,"startLine":1,"totalLines":2258}}}

The default implementation returns true.  */\n    90→  virtual bool gate (function *fun);\n    91→\n    92→  /* This is the code to run.  If this is not overridden, then there should\n    93→     be sub-passes otherwise this pass does nothing.\n    94→     The return value contains TODOs to execute in addition to those in\n    95→ 113→};\n   114→\n   115→/* Description of GIMPLE pass.  */\n   116→class gimple_opt_pass : public opt_pass\n   117→{\n   118→protected:\n   119→  gimple_opt_pass (const pass_data& data, gcc::context The second\n   161→     parameter is an array of statements indexed by their uid. */\n   162→  void (*stmt_fixup) (struct cgraph_node *, gimple **);\n   163→\n   164→  /* Results of interprocedural propagation of an IPA pass is applied to\n   165→     function body via this hook.  */\n   166→  unsigned int function_transform_todo_flags_start;\n   167→  unsigned int (*function_transform) (struct cgraph_node *);\n   168→  void (*variable_transform) (varpool_node *);\n   169→\n   170→protected:\n   171→  ipa_opt_pass_d (const pass_data& data, gcc::context *ctxt,\n   172→\t\t  void (*generate_summary) (void),\n   173→\t\t  void (*write_summary) (void),\n   174→\t\t  void (*read_summary) (void),\n   175→\t\t  void (*write_optimization_summary) (void),\n   176→\t\t  void (*read_optimization_summary) (void),\n   177→\t\t  void (*stmt_fixup) (struct cgraph_node *, gimple **),\n   178→\t\t  unsigned int function_transform_todo_flags_start,\n   179→\t\t  unsigned int (*function_transform) (struct cgraph_node *),\n   180→\t\t  void (*variable_transform) (varpool_node *))\n   181→    : opt_pass (data, ctxt),\n   182→      generate_summary (generate_summary),\n   183→      write_summary (write_summary),\n   184→      read_summary (read_summary),\n   185→      write_optimization_summary (write_optimization_summary),\n   186→      read_optimization_summary (read_optimization_summary),\n   187→      stmt_fixup (stmt_fixup),\n   188→      function_transform_todo_flags_start (function_transform_todo_flags_start),\n   189→      function_transform (function_transform),\n   190→      variable_transform (variable_transform)\n   191→  {\n   192→  }\n   193→};\n   194→\n   195→/* Description of simple IPA pass.  Simple IPA passes have just one execute\n   196→   hook.  */\n   197→class simple_ipa_opt_pass : public opt_pass\n   198→{\n   199→protected:\n   200→  simple_ipa_opt_pass (const pass_data& data, gcc::context *ctxt)\n   201→    : opt_pass (data, ctxt)\n   202→  {\n   203→  }\n   204→};\n   205→\n   206→/* Pass properties.  */\n   207→#define PROP_gimple_any\t\t(1 << 0)\t/* entire gimple grammar */\n   208→#define PROP_gimple_lcf\t\t(1 << 1)\t/* lowered control flow */\n   209→#define PROP_gimple_leh\t\t(1 << 2)\t/* lowered eh */\n   210→#define PROP_cfg\t\t(1 << 3)\n   211→#define PROP_objsz\t\t(1 << 4)\t/* object sizes computed */\n   212→#define PROP_ssa\t\t(1 << 5)\n   213→#define PROP_no_crit_edges      (1 << 6)\n   214→#define PROP_rtl\t\t(1 << 7)\n   215→#define PROP_gimple_lomp\t(1 << 8)\t/* lowered OpenMP directives */\n   216→#define PROP_cfglayout\t \t(1 << 9)\t/* cfglayout mode on RTL */\n   217→#define PROP_gimple_lcx\t\t(1 << 10)       /* lowered complex */\n   218→#define PROP_loops\t\t(1 << 11)\t/* preserve loop structures */\n   219→#define PROP_gimple_lvec\t(1 << 12)       /* lowered vector */\n   220→#define PROP_gimple_eomp\t(1 << 13)       /* no OpenMP directives */\n   221→#define PROP_gimple_lva\t\t(1 << 14)       /* No va_arg internal function.  */\n   222→#define PROP_gimple_opt_math\t(1 << 15)\t/* Disable canonicalization\n   223→\t\t\t\t\t\t   of math functions; the\n   224→\t\t\t\t\t\t   current choices have\n   225→\t\t\t\t\t\t   been optimized.  */\n   226→#define PROP_gimple_lomp_dev\t(1 << 16)\t/* done omp_device_lower */\n   227→#define PROP_rtl_split_insns\t(1 << 17)\t/* RTL has insns split.  */\n   228→#define PROP_loop_opts_done\t(1 << 18)\t/* SSA loop optimizations\n   229→\t\t\t\t\t\t   have completed.  */\n   230→#define PROP_assumptions_done\t(1 << 19)\t/* Assume function kept\n   231→\t\t\t\t\t\t   around.  */\n   232→#define PROP_gimple_lbitint\t(1 << 20)       /* lowered large _BitInt */\n   233→#define PROP_last_full_fold\t(1 << 21)\t/* Start of last forwprop.  */\n   234→\n   235→#define PROP_gimple \\\n   236→  (PROP_gimple_any | PROP_gimple_lcf | PROP_gimple_leh | PROP_gimple_lomp)\n   237→\n   238→/* To-do flags.  */\n   239→/* Note (1ul << 31) is reserved for TODO_verify_il. */\n   240→#define TODO_do_not_ggc_collect\t\t(1 << 1)\n   241→#define TODO_cleanup_cfg        \t(1 << 5)\n   242→#define TODO_dump_symtab\t\t(1 << 7)\n   243→#define TODO_remove_functions\t\t(1 << 8)\n   244→\n   245→/* To-do flags for calls to update_ssa.  */\n   246→\n   247→/* Update the SSA form inserting PHI nodes for newly exposed symbols\n   248→   and virtual names marked for updating.  When updating real names,\n   249→   only insert PHI nodes for a real name O_j in blocks reached by all\n   250→   the new and old definitions for O_j.  If the iterated dominance\n   251→   frontier for O_j is not pruned, we may end up inserting PHI nodes\n   252→   in blocks that have one or more edges with no incoming definition\n   253→   for O_j.  This would lead to uninitialized warnings for O_j's\n   254→   symbol.  */\n   255→#define TODO_update_ssa\t\t\t(1 << 11)\n   256→\n   257→/* Update the SSA form without inserting any new PHI nodes at all.\n   258→   This is used by passes that have either inserted all the PHI nodes\n   259→   themselves or passes that need only to patch use-def and def-def\n   260→   chains for virtuals (e.g., DCE).  */\n   261→#define TODO_update_ssa_no_phi\t\t(1 << 12)\n   262→\n   263→/* Insert PHI nodes everywhere they are needed.  No pruning of the\n   264→   IDF is done.  This is used by passes that need the PHI nodes for\n   265→   O_j even if it means that some arguments will come from the default\n   266→   definition of O_j's symbol.\n   267→\n   268→   WARNING: If you need to use this flag, chances are that your pass\n   269→   may be doing something wrong.  Inserting PHI nodes for an old name\n   270→   where not all edges carry a new replacement may lead to silent\n   271→   codegen errors or spurious uninitialized warnings.  */\n   272→#define TODO_update_ssa_full_phi\t(1 << 13)\n   273→\n   274→/* Passes that update the SSA form on their own may want to delegate\n   275→   the updating of virtual names to the generic updater.  Since FUD\n   276→   chains are easier to maintain, this simplifies the work they need\n   277→   to do.  NOTE: If this flag is used, any OLD->NEW mappings for real\n   278→   names are explicitly destroyed and only the symbols marked for\n   279→   renaming are processed.  */\n   280→#define TODO_update_ssa_only_virtuals\t(1 << 14)\n   281→\n   282→/* Some passes leave unused local variables that can be removed from\n   283→   cfun->local_decls.  This reduces the size of dump files\n   284→   and the memory footprint for VAR_DECLs.  */\n   285→#define TODO_remove_unused_locals\t(1 << 15)\n   286→\n   287→/* Call df_finish at the end of the pass.  This is done after all of\n   288→   the dumpers have been allowed to run so that they have access to\n   289→   the instance before it is destroyed.  */\n   290→#define TODO_df_finish                  (1 << 17)\n   291→\n   292→/* Call df_verify at the end of the pass if checking is enabled.  */\n   293→#define TODO_df_verify                  (1 << 18)\n   294→\n   295→/* Internally used for the first instance of a pass.  */\n   296→#define TODO_mark_first_instance\t(1 << 19)\n   297→\n   298→/* Rebuild aliasing info.  */\n   299→#define TODO_rebuild_alias              (1 << 20)\n   300→\n   301→/* Rebuild the addressable-vars bitmap and do register promotion.  */\n   302→#define TODO_update_address_taken\t(1 << 21)\n   303→\n   304→/* Rebuild the callgraph edges.  */\n   305→#define TODO_rebuild_cgraph_edges       (1 << 22)\n   306→\n   307→/* Release function body (unless assumption function)\n   308→   and stop pass manager.  */\n   309→#define TODO_discard_function\t\t(1 << 23)\n   310→\n   311→/* (1ul << 31) is reserved for TODO_verify_il. */\n   312→\n   313→/* Internally used in execute_function_todo().  */\n   314→#define TODO_update_ssa_any\t\t\\\n   315→    (TODO_update_ssa\t\t\t\\\n   316→     | TODO_update_ssa_no_phi\t\t\\\n   317→     | TODO_update_ssa_full_phi\t\t\\\n   318→     | TODO_update_ssa_only_virtuals)\n   319→\n   320→/* To-do flags for pending_TODOs.  */\n   321→\n   322→/* Tell the next scalar cleanup pass that there is\n   323→   work for it to do.  */\n   324→#define PENDING_TODO_force_next_scalar_cleanup  (1 << 1)\n   325→\n   326→/* Register pass info. */\n   327→\n   328→enum pass_positioning_ops\n   329→{\n   330→  PASS_POS_INSERT_AFTER,  /* Insert after the reference pass.  */\n   331→  PASS_POS_INSERT_BEFORE, /* Insert before the reference pass.  */\n   332→  PASS_POS_REPLACE        /* Replace the reference pass.  */\n   333→};\n   334→\n   335→struct register_pass_info\n   336→{\n   337→  opt_pass *pass;\t\t    /* New pass to register.  */\n   338→  const char *reference_pass_name;  /* Name of the reference pass for hooking\n   339→                                       up the new pass.  */\n   340→  int ref_pass_instance_number;     /* Insert the pass at the specified\n   341→                                       instance number of the reference pass.\n   342→                                       Do it for every instance if it is 0.  */\n   343→  enum pass_positioning_ops pos_op; /* how to insert the new pass.  */\n   344→};\n   345→\n   346→/* Registers a new pass.  Either fill out the register_pass_info or specify\n   347→   the individual parameters.  The pass object is expected to have been\n   348→   allocated using operator new and the pass manager takes the ownership of\n   349→   the pass object.  */\n   350→extern void register_pass (register_pass_info *);\n   351→extern void register_pass (opt_pass* pass, pass_positioning_ops pos,\n   352→\t\t\t   const char* ref_pass_name, int ref_pass_inst_number);\n   353→\n   354→extern
